 input:ians Aruna Ramchandra Shanbag, who has been living in a single bed in 37 years at King Edward Memorial (KEM) Hospital in Mumbai, will have to live, and will not get euthanasia
 haalanki supreme court ne somvaar ko apane bahupratikshit faisle main vyavastha di he ki asaadhaaran paristhitiyon main rogi ko 'pasive yuthensia' (aisi mrityu, jisamen rogi kaa ilaaj roak diya jaae yaa use jeevanarakshak upkarnon se hataa liya jaae) kii anumati di ja sakati he, lekin 'active yuthensia' (aisi mrityu, jisamen rogi kaa jivan injection ityadi dekar khatm kar diya jaae) avaidh he
 On Monday, a bench of Justice Markandey Katju and Justice Gyan Sudha Mishra dismissed a petition filed by Ninky Aruna on behalf of Nurse Aruna, who wrote a book on her life, stating that the facts, circumstances, medical evidence and others in the case presented The material suggests that the victim does not need euthanasia
 supreme court dwaara aruna ke maamle main sunaae gaye is nirnay se ab hamaara desh bhi un mulkon kii fehrist main darj ho gaya he, jahaan kisi na kisi rup main ichhamrityu vaid he
 The bench, however, also said that since at present there is no law regarding euthanasia in our country, a patient with a dying condition can be allowed to have passive euthanasia in 'exceptional cases'
 peeth ne spasht kiya ki jab tak sansad ise lekar koi kanoon nahin banaati, yah faisla ichhamrityu ke donon tareekon (active or pasive yuthensia) par lagu rahegaa tathaa pasive yuthensia ke liye bhi hoicourt se sweekruti lenaa anivaary hoga
 To allow passive euthanasia, the bench clarified that in the absence of the patient's parents, spouse, other relatives or close relatives, a close friend or a treating doctor may decide to remove life-saving equipment or treatment, so Aruna's The KEM hospital staff, who has been treating and caring for the past several decades, has the right to make this decision in the case
 adaalat ne kaha ki aspataal kaa staff chahta he ki aruna ko jeene diya jaae, isliye yachikakarta ko aruna kii zindagi ke bare main nirnay lene kaa adhikaar nahin he
 The court also clarified that if the KEM Hospital staff also changes its mind in future, then it will have to seek permission from the Bombay High Court
 ullekhneey he ki aspataal kii ore se prastut vakil vallabh sisodiya ne yachika ko virodh karte hue adaalat ko jaankaree di thi ki aspatalkarmi, visheshkar aruna kii ilaaj or timaardaari kar rahe doctor or norsen pichley 37 saal se kaaphi acha kaam kar rahe hai or ve use maare jane ke aagrah ke viruddh hai
 It is noteworthy that at this time Aruna, who has turned 60, was brutally raped by a sanitation worker at the hospital on 27 November 1973
 yachikakarta ne court ko jaankaree di ki aspataal ke ek safaikarmi ne aruna ke gale main kute kii chen lapetakar jhatak diya tha, jisase vah coma main chali gai thi
 According to the petition, the rapist tried to rape Aruna, but as her menstruation continued, she raped Aruna unnaturally
 aruna kii ore se virodh ko rokane ke liye aaropee ne uske gale main chen lapetakar jhatka diya tha
 After committing this heinous crime, the accused escaped from the spot
 yachikakarta ne bataaya ki galaa ghut jane se aruna ke mastishk ko oxigen kii aapurti band ho gai or uskaa cartex kshatigrast hua
 Due to this attack, there was internal injury to Aruna's cervical cord as well as brain ducts
 yachikakarta ke mutabik vaardaat ke baad pichley 37 saal main aruna kaa vajan behad kam ho gaya he or uski haddiyaan charmara chuki hai
 Due to lying in bed, his skin has also got infected, his wrists have turned inward, teeth have been destroyed and he can only be given chilled food
 unhone kaha ki aruna lagaataar behoshee kii haalat main he, uskaa mastishk asal main mrit ho chukaa he or use duniya kii koi sud nahin he
